<script type="text/javascript">
                Dropzone.autoDiscover = false;
            </script>
<div class="modal-header">

<p class="modal-spacing"><span class="fontOrange">NOTE:</span> Every APK file is manually reviewed by the <a href="http://www.androidpolice.com" target="_blank">AndroidPolice</a> team before being posted to the site.</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
                var myDropzone;

                var uploadrequested = false;

                var files_state = [];
                var files = [];
                var STATE_IDLE = 0;
                var STATE_CHECKING = 1;
                var STATE_CHECKED = 2;
                var STATE_UPLOADING = 3;
                var STATE_SUCCESS = 4;
                var STATE_FAIL = 5;

                initDropzone();

                //Load the cookie data
                jQuery("#fullname").val(getCookie("apkmirror_name"));
                jQuery("#email").val(getCookie("apkmirror_email"));
                updateUI();

                jQuery('#uploadAPK').on('hide.bs.modal', function (e) {
                    resetForm();

                    if (location.hash == "#" + this.id){
                        history.replaceState('', document.title, window.location.pathname);
                        history.back();
                    }
                });

                jQuery('#uploadAPK').on('show.bs.modal', function () {
                    var modal = this;
                    var hash = modal.id;
                    window.location.hash = hash;
                    window.onhashchange = function() {
                        if (!location.hash){
                            jQuery(modal).modal('hide');
                        }
                    }
                });

                jQuery(document).on('keydown', function(e) {
                    if (e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() !== 'input' &&
                        e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() !== 'textarea') {
                        if((e.keyCode == 27) && (jQuery('#uploadAPK').hasClass('in'))){ //esc
                            history.back();
                        }
                        if(e.keyCode == 8){ //backspace
                            //    jQuery('#uploadAPK').modal('hide');
                        }
                    }
                });

                function initDropzone()
                {
                    // Get the template HTML and remove it from the doumenthe template HTML and remove it from the doument
                    var templateNode = document.querySelector("#row-template");
                    templateNode.id = "";
                    var rowTemplate = templateNode.parentNode.innerHTML;
                    templateNode.parentNode.removeChild(templateNode);

                    myDropzone = new Dropzone(document.body, {
                        maxFilesize: 2000,
                        url: "//www.apkmirror.com/wp-content/plugins/UploadManager/inc/upload.php",
                        previewTemplate: rowTemplate,
                        dictResponseError: "An error occurred!",
                        previewsContainer: "#myDropZone",
                        clickable: ".uploadAreaTable",
                        autoProcessQueue: false,
                        acceptedFiles: '.apk,.APK',
                        maxFiles: 25,
                        parallelUploads: 1});

                    myDropzone.on("dragenter", function(event){
                                                jQuery('#uploadAPK').modal('show');
                                            });

                    myDropzone.on("complete", function(){
                        updateUI();
                    });

                    myDropzone.on("sending", function(file, xhr, formData){
                        var index = files.indexOf(file);
                        if(index > -1){
                            files_state[index] = STATE_UPLOADING;
                        }

                        //Append form fields
                        var nameField = document.getElementById("fullname");
                        var emailField = document.getElementById("email");
                        var changesField = document.getElementById("changes");

                        formData.append("fullname", nameField.value);
                        formData.append("email", emailField.value);
                        formData.append("changes", changesField.value);
                        formData.append("_wpnonce", 'b89c04f0a7');

                        updateUI();
                    });

                    myDropzone.on("addedfile", function(file){
                        //Add new file to state list
                        files_state.push(STATE_IDLE);
                        files.push(file);
                        var currentindex = files_state.length - 1;

                        if (file.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(".apk") > -1) {
                            // Check md5 for this file
                            // Check for the various File API support.
                            if (window.File && window.FileReader && window.FileList && window.Blob) {
                                // Great success! All the File APIs are supported.
                                // Only check md5 if browser supports it
                                console.log("start md5");
                                files_state[currentindex] = STATE_CHECKING;
                                updateUI();

                                var hash = md5.create();
                                var chunk_size = 10 * 1024 * 1024; //10MB
                                var start = 0;
                                var stop = 0;

                                stop = chunk_size - 1;
                                if (stop > (file.size - 1)) {
                                    stop = (file.size - 1);
                                }

                                // Read file
                                var reader = new FileReader();
                                reader.onloadend = function (evt) {
                                    if (evt.target.readyState == FileReader.DONE) { // DONE == 2
                                        hash.update(evt.target.result);

                                        //Move onto next chunk
                                        if (stop != (file.size - 1)) {
                                            start = stop + 1;

                                            stop = stop + chunk_size;
                                            if (stop > (file.size - 1)) {
                                                stop = (file.size - 1);
                                            }

                                            var blob = file.slice(start, stop + 1);
                                            reader.readAsArrayBuffer(blob);
                                        }
                                        else {
                                            //We are done
                                            console.log("end md5");

                                            //Confirm with server if this is a new file
                                            jQuery.getJSON( "/wp-json/apkm/v1/apk_uploadable/" + hash.hex()).done(function(result) {
                                                if(result){
                                                    if(result.status != "uploadable") {
                                                        var return_msg = '';
                                                        if (result.status == "dupe") {
                                                            if (result.link.length !== 0) {
                                                                return_msg = "Thanks, but we already have this APK on the website: <a href=\"" + result.link + "\">" + result.title + "</a>!";
                                                            } else {
                                                                return_msg = "Thanks, but we already have this APK on the website!";
                                                            }
                                                            console.log("APK already exists");
                                                        }
                                                        else if (result.status == "similar") {
                                                            if (result.link.length !== 0) {
                                                                return_msg = "Thanks, but we already have a similar APK on the website: <a href=\"" + result.link + "\">" + result.title + "</a>!";
                                                            } else {
                                                                return_msg = "Thanks, but we already have a similar APK on the website!";
                                                            }
                                                            console.log("APK already exists");
                                                        }
                                                        else if(result.status == "blacklisted")
                                                        {
                                                            return_msg = result.reason;
                                                            console.log("APK blacklisted: " + result.reason);
                                                        }

                                                        var targetDiv = file.previewElement.getElementsByClassName('dz-error-message')[0];
                                                        targetDiv.innerHTML = return_msg;

                                                        var targetDiv = file.previewElement.getElementsByClassName('dz-remove')[0];
                                                        targetDiv.innerHTML = '';

                                                        var previewElementJquery = jQuery(file.previewElement);
                                                        previewElementJquery.removeClass('dz-success');
                                                        previewElementJquery.addClass('dz-error');

                                                        file.status = Dropzone.ERROR;

                                                        files_state[currentindex] = STATE_FAIL;
                                                        updateUI();
                                                    }
                                                    else{
                                                        console.log("APK is new");
                                                        files_state[currentindex] = STATE_CHECKED;
                                                        updateUI();
                                                    }
                                                }else{
                                                    files_state[currentindex] = STATE_CHECKED;
                                                    updateUI();
                                                }
                                            })
                                                .fail(function( jqxhr, status, error) {
                                                    //Check failed (server error, not found, etc.), continue upload
                                                    files_state[currentindex] = STATE_CHECKED;
                                                    updateUI();
                                                });
                                        }
                                    }
                                };

                                //First blob
                                var blob = file.slice(start, stop + 1);
                                reader.readAsArrayBuffer(blob);
                            }else {
                                //No file APIs supported
                                files_state[currentindex] = STATE_CHECKED; //Skip the md5 check
                                updateUI();
                            }
                        }
                        else{
                            //Not an APK?
                            files_state[currentindex] = STATE_FAIL;
                            updateUI();
                        }
                    });
                    myDropzone.on("removedfile", function(file){
                        //Remove the file from our indices
                        var index = files.indexOf(file);
                        if(index > -1){
                            files.splice(index, 1);
                            files_state.splice(index, 1);
                        }

                        updateUI();
                    });

                    // Update the total progress bar
                    myDropzone.on("totaluploadprogress", function(progress) {
                        //jQuery("#total-upload-progress").width(progress + "%");
                    });

                    // Update the individual progress bar
                    myDropzone.on("uploadprogress", function(file, progress) {
                        jQuery("#file-upload-progress").width(progress + "%");

                        var idle_count = 0;
                        var checking_count = 0;
                        var checked_count = 0;
                        var uploading_count = 0;
                        var success_count = 0;
                        var fail_count = 0;

                        for(var i = 0; i < files_state.length; i++){
                            switch(files_state[i]){
                                case STATE_IDLE:
                                    idle_count++;
                                    break;
                                case STATE_CHECKING:
                                    checking_count++;
                                    break;
                                case STATE_CHECKED:
                                    checked_count++;
                                    break;
                                case STATE_UPLOADING:
                                    uploading_count++;
                                    break;
                                case STATE_SUCCESS:
                                    success_count++;
                                    break;
                                case STATE_FAIL:
                                    fail_count++;
                                    break;
                            }
                        }
                        var total_count = idle_count + checking_count + checked_count + uploading_count + success_count + fail_count;

                        var totalprogress = ((success_count + fail_count) / total_count) * 100;

                        jQuery("#total-upload-progress").width(totalprogress + "%");
                    });

                    myDropzone.on("error", function(file, serverresponse) {
                        //Update status array
                        var index = files.indexOf(file);
                        if(index > -1) {
                            files_state[index] = STATE_FAIL;
                        }

                        var targetDiv = file.previewElement.getElementsByClassName('dz-error-message')[0];
                        if(serverresponse != ""){
                            targetDiv.innerHTML = serverresponse;
                        }else{
                            targetDiv.innerHTML = "Sorry, your upload might have failed somewhere. Please try again.";
                        }
                        var targetDiv = file.previewElement.getElementsByClassName('dz-remove')[0];
                        targetDiv.innerHTML = '';

                        updateUI();
                    });

                    myDropzone.on("success", function(file, serverresponse) {
                        if(serverresponse != "UPLOADOK"){
                            var index = files.indexOf(file);
                            if(index > -1){
                                files_state[index] = STATE_FAIL;
                            }

                            var targetDiv = file.previewElement.getElementsByClassName('dz-error-message')[0];
                            targetDiv.innerHTML = "Sorry, your upload might have failed somewhere. Please try again.";
                            var targetDiv = file.previewElement.getElementsByClassName('dz-remove')[0];
                            targetDiv.innerHTML = '';
                            var previewElementJquery = jQuery(file.previewElement);
                            previewElementJquery.removeClass('dz-success');
                            previewElementJquery.addClass('dz-error');
                        }else{
                            var index = files.indexOf(file);
                            if(index > -1){
                                files_state[index] = STATE_SUCCESS;
                            }
                        }

                        updateUI();
                    });
                }

                function updateUI(){
                    var idle_count = 0;
                    var checking_count = 0;
                    var checked_count = 0;
                    var uploading_count = 0;
                    var success_count = 0;
                    var fail_count = 0;

                    for(var i = 0; i < files_state.length; i++){
                        switch(files_state[i]){
                            case STATE_IDLE:
                                idle_count++;
                                break;
                            case STATE_CHECKING:
                                checking_count++;
                                break;
                            case STATE_CHECKED:
                                checked_count++;
                                break;
                            case STATE_UPLOADING:
                                uploading_count++;
                                break;
                            case STATE_SUCCESS:
                                success_count++;
                                break;
                            case STATE_FAIL:
                                fail_count++;
                                break;
                        }
                    }

                    var total_count = idle_count + checking_count + checked_count + uploading_count + success_count + fail_count;

                    //Start uploading again when files are added and an upload is in progress
                    if(idle_count + checking_count + checked_count > 0 && uploading_count > 0){
                        uploadrequested = true;
                    }

                    //Start upload as soon as files are ready to be uploaded and nothing is currently uploading.
                    if(idle_count + checking_count + uploading_count == 0 && uploadrequested){
                        uploadrequested = false;

                        if(checked_count > 0) {
                            myDropzone.processQueue();
                            return;
                        }
                    }

                    //Hide the upload cloud if there are any files in the queue
                    if(total_count > 0){
                        jQuery(".uploadCloud").hide();
                    }else{
                        jQuery(".uploadCloud").show();
                    }

                    //Show close only when queue is done (only successes and fails) and when there are no files at all
                    if((idle_count + checked_count + checking_count > 0 && uploading_count == 0) || ((idle_count + checked_count + checking_count + uploading_count == 0) && (success_count + fail_count > 0)) || total_count == 0){
                        //Show cancel only when queue is busy with something (uploading), or upload has been requested
                        if(uploading_count > 0 || uploadrequested){
                            jQuery("#btnDismiss").show().text("Cancel").removeClass("disabled");
                        }else{
                            jQuery("#btnDismiss").show().text("Close").removeClass("disabled");
                        }
                    }else{
                        //Show cancel only when queue is busy with something (uploading), or upload has been requested
                        if(uploading_count > 0 || uploadrequested){
                            jQuery("#btnDismiss").show().text("Cancel").removeClass("disabled");
                        }else{
                            jQuery("#btnDismiss").show().text("Close").addClass("disabled");
                        }
                    }




                    //Show upload only when files have been added and are not uploading yet and no upload has been requested
                    if(idle_count + checking_count + checked_count > 0 && !uploadrequested && uploading_count == 0){
                        jQuery("#btnSubmit").show().removeClass('disabled');
                    }else{
                        jQuery("#btnSubmit").show().addClass('disabled');

                    }

                    //Show success banner when there are files with success, and nothing is currently uploading or added
                    if(success_count > 0 && (idle_count + checking_count + checked_count + uploading_count == 0)){
                        jQuery("#success-message-bar").show("fast");
                    }else{
                        jQuery("#success-message-bar").hide("fast");
                    }

                    //Show error banner when there are files with errors
                    if(fail_count > 0 && (idle_count + checking_count + checked_count + uploading_count == 0)){
                        jQuery("#errorMessage").text("Some APKs had problems uploading.");
                        jQuery("#error-message-bar").show("fast");
                    }else{
                        jQuery("#error-message-bar").hide("fast");
                    }

                    //Show upload progress when there are files being uploaded
                    if(uploading_count > 0){
                        jQuery(".upload-progress").slideDown('fast');
                    }else{
                        jQuery(".upload-progress").slideUp('fast');
                    }
                }

                function uploadFilesSubmit() {
                    if(!jQuery("#btnSubmit").hasClass('disabled')) {

                        //Check if all fields have been filled out
                        var nameField = document.getElementById("fullname");
                        var emailField = document.getElementById("email");
                        var changesField = document.getElementById("changes");

                        jQuery("#error-message-bar").hide("fast");

                        if (nameField.value == "") {
                            jQuery("#errorMessage").text("Please enter your name.");
                            jQuery("#error-message-bar").show("fast");
                        }
                        else if (!validateEmail(emailField.value)) {
                            jQuery("#errorMessage").text("Please enter a valid email address.");
                            jQuery("#error-message-bar").show("fast");
                        }
                        else {
                            //Save data in cookies
                            setCookie("apkmirror_name", nameField.value, 1000);
                            setCookie("apkmirror_email", emailField.value, 1000);

                            uploadrequested = true;
                            updateUI();
                        }
                    }
                }

                function validateEmail(email) {
                    var re = /^(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
                    return re.test(email);
                }

                function resetForm()
                {
                    if(!jQuery("#btnDismiss").hasClass("disabled")) {
                        myDropzone.removeAllFiles(true);

                        var changesField = document.getElementById("changes");
                        changesField.value = "";

                        files_state.length = 0;
                        files.length = 0;
                        updateUI();
                    }
                }



                function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
                    var d = new Date();
                    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
                    var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
                    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires + ";path=/";
                }

                function getCookie(cname) {
                    var name = cname + "=";
                    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
                        var c = ca[i];
                        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
                        if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
                    }
                    return "";
                }

            </script>

        //Loading these in-line to ensure the buttons work as soon as possible

        //Perform Search button
        jQuery(".searchButton:visible").first().on('click', function() {
            performSearch();
        })
        jQuery("#searchbutton-mobile").on('click', function() {
            performSearch();
        })

        function performSearch() {
            //If the search filter form is present (i.e. we are on the search page), submit that form instead
            if (jQuery('#apkm-search-filters').length !== 0) {
                jQuery("#apply-search-form").click();
            } else {
                var searchquery = jQuery(".searchbox:visible").first().val();
                jQuery('#search-form').append('<input type="hidden" name="s" value="' + searchquery + '" /> ');
                document.forms["search-form"].submit();
            }
        }

        jQuery(".searchbox:visible").first().on('keypress', function (e) {
            if(e.which === 13){
                performSearch();
            }
        });
        jQuery("#searchbox-mobile").on('keypress', function (e) {
            if(e.which === 13){
                performSearch();
            }
        });

        //Search filter icon
        jQuery(".search-filter-button:visible").first().on('click', function() {
            filterButtonClick();
        });

        //Search filter icon
        jQuery("#searchfilter-button-mobile").on('click', function() {
            filterButtonClick();
        });

        function filterButtonClick() {
            //If the search filter form is present (i.e. we are on the search page), just toggle the panel
            if (jQuery('#apkm-search-filters').length !== 0) {
                jQuery('.advanced-search-container').toggle();
                jQuery('#advanced-searched-caret').toggleClass('dropup');
            } else {
                jQuery('#search-form').append('<input type="hidden" name="filter" value="true" /> ');
                jQuery('#apkm-search-searchtype').val('apk');
                jQuery(".searchButton:visible").first().click();
            }
        }

        //Search cancel button X
        jQuery("#backButton").on('click', function() {
            if(searchOn){
                //Hide search bar
                jQuery("#hamburgerMenu").show();
                jQuery("#mobileSearch").addClass('hidden');
                jQuery("#mobileDefault").removeClass('hidden');
                jQuery(".siteTitle").show();
                jQuery(".siteImage").show();
                searchOn = false;
                jQuery("#searchbox-mobile").val('');
            }
        });

        //Hamburger menu button
        var menuOn = false;
        jQuery("#hamburgerMenu").on('click', function() {
            if(!menuOn){
                if(searchOn){
                    //Hide search bar
                    jQuery("#hamburgerMenu").show();
                    jQuery("#mobileSearch").addClass('hidden');
                    jQuery("#mobileDefault").removeClass('hidden');
                    jQuery(".siteTitle").show();
                    jQuery(".siteImage").show();
                    searchOn = false;
                    jQuery("#searchbox-mobile").val('');
                }
                //Show menu
                menuOn = true;
                jQuery("#mobile-slide-menu").animate({left:'0px'}, "fast");
                jQuery("#cover-screen").show();
                jQuery("#cover-screen").animate({opacity:'0.6'}, "fast");
            }else{
                menuOn = false;
                jQuery("#mobile-slide-menu").animate({left:'-310px'}, "fast");
                jQuery("#cover-screen").hide();
                jQuery("#cover-screen").animate({opacity:'0'}, "fast");

            }
        });

        //Mobile search button
        var searchOn = false;
        jQuery("#searchButtonMobile").on('click', function() {
            if(!searchOn){
                if(menuOn){
                    //Close slideout menu
                    menuOn = false;
                    jQuery("#mobile-slide-menu").animate({left:'-310px'}, "fast");
                    jQuery("#cover-screen").hide();
                    jQuery("#cover-screen").animate({opacity:'0'}, "fast");
                }
                //Show search bar
                jQuery("#hamburgerMenu").hide();
                jQuery("#mobileSearch").removeClass('hidden');
                jQuery("#mobileDefault").addClass('hidden');
                jQuery(".siteTitle").hide();
                jQuery(".siteImage").hide();

                //Set focus on search box to trigger keyboard
                jQuery("#searchbox-mobile").focus();
                searchOn = true;
            }
        });

        //Info button and info panel dropdown code
        var lastClicked = "";
        function infoButtonClick(item) {
            if(lastClicked != item)
            {
                jQuery('.infoSlide').slideUp('fast');
                jQuery('.infoLink').removeClass('activated');
                jQuery('svg.info-icon').css('color', '');
                jQuery(item).addClass('activated');
                jQuery(item).parents(".appRow").nextAll(".infoSlide").first().slideDown('fast');
                jQuery(item).find('.info-icon').css('color', jQuery(item).data('accent-color'));
                lastClicked = item;
            }
            else
            {
                //Close the same one
                jQuery('.infoSlide').slideUp('fast');
                jQuery('.infoLink').removeClass('activated');
                jQuery('svg.info-icon').css('color', '');
                lastClicked = "";
            }

            return false;
        }

        var lastDevClicked = "";

        function infoDevButtonClick(item) {
            if(lastDevClicked != item)
            {
                jQuery('.infoDevSlide').slideUp('fast');
                jQuery('.infoSlide').slideUp('fast');
                jQuery('.infoDevLink').removeClass('activated');
                jQuery(item).addClass('activated');
                jQuery(item).parents(".appRow").find(".infoDevSlide").slideDown('fast');
                lastDevClicked = item;
            }
            else
            {
                //Close the same one
                jQuery('.infoDevSlide').slideUp('fast');
                jQuery('.infoDevLink').removeClass('activated');
                lastDevClicked = "";
            }

            return false;
        }
    </script>

<div class="notes wrapText"><p>NEW! Now you can battle other Pokémon GO Trainers online! Try the GO Battle League today!</p>
<p>Join Trainers across the globe who are discovering Pokémon as they explore the world around them. Pokémon GO is the global gaming sensation that has been downloaded over 1 billion times and named “Best Mobile Game” by the Game Developers Choice Awards and “Best App of the Year” by TechCrunch.<br>
_______________</p>
<p>UNCOVER THE WORLD OF POKÉMON: Explore and discover Pokémon wherever you are!</p>
<p>CATCH more Pokémon to complete your Pokédex!</p>
<p>JOURNEY alongside your Buddy Pokémon to help make your Pokémon stronger and earn rewards!</p>
<p>COMPETE in epic Gym battles and...</p>
<p>TEAM UP with other Trainers to catch powerful Pokémon during Raid Battles!</p>
<p>It’s time to get moving—your real-life adventures await! Let’s GO!<br>
_______________</p>
<p>Notes:<br>
- This app is free-to-play and offers in-game purchases. It is optimized for smartphones, not tablets.<br>
- Compatible with Android devices that have 2GB RAM or more and have Android Version 6.0–10.0+ installed.<br>
- Compatibility is not guaranteed for devices without GPS capabilities or devices that are connected only to Wi-Fi networks.<br>
- Application may not run on certain devices even if they have compatible OS versions installed.<br>
- It is recommended to play while connected to a network in order to obtain accurate location information.<br>
- Compatibility information may be changed at any time.<br>
- Please visit PokemonGO.com for additional compatibility information.<br>
- Information current as of October 20, 2020.</p>

    var ranTwice = false;

    function pvkYfPbFwM() {
        var visibleAds = 0;
        jQuery(".gooWidget > .adsbygoogle" ).each(function( i ) {
            if (jQuery(this).is(':visible') && jQuery(this).children().length > 0) {
                visibleAds += 1;
            }
        });
        console.log("Visible ads: " + visibleAds);

        var canRunAds = false;
        if(visibleAds >= 2) { canRunAds = true; } else { canRunAds = false;}

        if(jQuery(".downloadButton").length > 0) {
            if(canRunAds == true)
            {
                jQuery(".downloadButton").removeClass("disabled");
            }
            else
            {
                var elapsedTime = 0;
                var totalTime = 15;
                jQuery(".downloadButton").addClass("disabled");
                jQuery(".downloadCountdown").show();

                //Ad blocker is running for sure, show the countdown
                var timerInterval = setInterval(function() {
                    elapsedTime += 1;
                    var timeLeft = totalTime - elapsedTime;

                    jQuery("#secondsLeft").text(timeLeft);

                    if(timeLeft == 1)
                    {
                        jQuery("#secondsPlural").text("second");
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        jQuery("#secondsPlural").text("seconds");
                    }

                    if(elapsedTime >= totalTime) {
                        elapsedTime = totalTime;
                        jQuery(".downloadCountdown").slideUp("slow");
                        jQuery(".downloadButton").removeClass("disabled");
                        clearInterval( timerInterval );
                    }

                }, 1000);

                jQuery("#downloadCountdownBar").width("100%");
            }

            if(canRunAds == false) {
                jQuery("#sidebar .latestWidget").css("margin-top", "0px");
            }

            if(canRunAds && !ranTwice)
            {
                ranTwice = true;
            }
        }
    }

    jQuery(window).on('load', function() { pvkYfPbFwM(); });
</script>
